  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_f55f4afe-2880-4424-8254-8d8047f21579'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer6244192124909280721">The universe of the Lunar Chronicles holds stories—and secrets—that are wondrous, vicious, and romantic. How did Cinder first arrive in New Beijing? How did the brooding soldier Wolf transform from young man to killer? When did Princess Winter and the palace guard Jacin realize their destinies? With nine stories—five of which have never before been published—and an excerpt</span>
  <span id="freeText6244192124909280721" style="display:none">The universe of the Lunar Chronicles holds stories—and secrets—that are wondrous, vicious, and romantic. How did Cinder first arrive in New Beijing? How did the brooding soldier Wolf transform from young man to killer? When did Princess Winter and the palace guard Jacin realize their destinies? With nine stories—five of which have never before been published—and an excerpt from Marissa Meyer’s novel, Heartless, about the Queen of Hearts from Alice in Wonderland, Stars Above is essential for fans of the bestselling and beloved Lunar Chronicles. <br /><br /><u>CONTENTS</u><br /><b>The Keeper:</b> A prequel to the Lunar Chronicles, showing a young Scarlet and how Princess Selene came into the care of Michelle Benoit. <br /><b>Glitches:</b> In this prequel to Cinder, we see the results of the plague play out, and the emotional toll it takes on Cinder. Something that may, or may not, be a glitch…. <br /><b>The Queen’s Army:</b> In this prequel to Scarlet, we’re introduced to the army Queen Levana is building, and one soldier in particular who will do anything to keep from becoming the monster they want him to be. <br /><b>Carswell’s Guide to Being Lucky:</b> Thirteen-year-old Carswell Thorne has big plans involving a Rampion spaceship and a no-return trip out of Los Angeles. <br /><b>After Sunshine Passes By:</b> In this prequel to Cress, we see how a nine-year-old Cress ended up alone on a satellite, spying on Earth for Luna. <br /><b>The Princess and the Guard:</b> In this prequel to Winter, we see a young Winter and Jacin playing a game called the Princess and the Guard… <br /><b>The Little Android:</b> A retelling of Hans Christian Andersen’s “The Little Mermaid,” set in the world of The Lunar Chronicles. <br /><b>The Mechanic:</b> In this prequel to Cinder, we see Kai and Cinder’s first meeting from Kai’s perspective. <br /><b>Something Old, Something New:</b> In this epilogue to Winter, friends gather for the wedding of the century…</span>
  <a data-text-id="6244192124909280721" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>
</div>

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

        $('edition_34511898').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('edition_34511898').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('edition_34511898').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);

        });

<div id="review_1741314666" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1741314666" />

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina">Katerina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=dystopia">dystopia</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=retellings">retellings</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1741314666" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4592920484778553975"><b>And they lived happily ever after.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472398686ra/20189345.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Except the girl-who-read-too-much, aka Katerina, since <b>she cried her eyes out</b>, sniffled, hiccupped and then cried some more.<br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“The first time, he had wondered why she liked books so much, and if it had anything to do with why he liked spaceships. Because they could take you somewhere far, far away.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>But mind that they were <b>happy tears</b> (mostly). The tears you shed when your babies that went through pain and difficulties find <b>love, happiness, joy and fri</b></span>
  <span id="freeText4592920484778553975" style="display:none"><b>And they lived happily ever after.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472398686ra/20189345.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Except the girl-who-read-too-much, aka Katerina, since <b>she cried her eyes out</b>, sniffled, hiccupped and then cried some more.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“The first time, he had wondered why she liked books so much, and if it had anything to do with why he liked spaceships. Because they could take you somewhere far, far away.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>But mind that they were <b>happy tears</b> (mostly). The tears you shed when your babies that went through pain and difficulties find <b>love, happiness, joy and friendship</b>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472398686ra/20189346.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“That mechanic was going to change everything.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>Thank the stars above that <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4684322.Marissa_Meyer" title="Marissa Meyer" rel="nofollow noopener">Marissa Meyer</a> decided to write these novellas</b> and gave us more precious moments with the characters we came to cherish, before the closure and the aforementioned tears happened. With <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25689074.Stars_Above__The_Lunar_Chronicles___4_5_" title="Stars Above (The Lunar Chronicles, #4.5) by Marissa Meyer" rel="nofollow noopener">Stars Above</a> my heart, the heart that was bruised and beaten and bet rapidly and sighed with contentment while reading The Lunar Chronicles, was so <b>full of love that my chest nearly exploded</b>! I experienced <b>pain</b> with The Little Andoid and The Queen's Army, because the first one was really <b>touching</b> and the second narrated how Wolf tried to not become the monster everyone expected him to, and I wanted so badly to hug him and tell him about the red-haired girl that would become his alpha and his home. I <b>laughed</b> with 13-years-old Thorne that charmed everyone with his good looks and flirtatious ways and was dedicated to his goals. I devoured every single story about the past of Rampion's crew that made me understand better my heroes and share their sorrows and misfortunes and admire the strong people they became! But let's be honest, the last story, the fairytale wedding, was what left me giggling while wiping away my tears!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472401420ra/20189764.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You are the most beautiful sight I have ever laid eyes on.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>A full circle that came to an end. There is no need for hot make-out sessions and sexual innuendos to create a romance that will make your chest burst. Just the connection between two souls, the acceptance and the efforts to overcome every obstacle. And <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4684322.Marissa_Meyer" title="Marissa Meyer" rel="nofollow noopener">Marissa Meyer</a>, with her <b>stardust</b> and <b>beautiful soul</b>, created not one, not two but four great love stories that restored my faith in magic and happily ever afters.<br><br><b>Cinder.<br>Kai.<br>Wolf.<br>Scarlet.<br>Cress. <br>Thorne.<br>Winter.<br>Jacin.<br><br>Marissa.<br><br>It has been the privilege and the honor of my life to know and love you.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472401420ra/20189765.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>✨ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1183237483?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Cinder review</a><br>✨ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1183237129?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Scarlet review</a><br>✨ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1183237156?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Cress review</a><br>✨ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1153134052?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Winter review</a></span>

<div id="review_2253667910" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2253667910" />
    <a title="Miranda Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/71848701-miranda-reads"><img alt="Miranda Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1592243041p2/71848701.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2253667910?book_show_action=true">Feb 06, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Miranda Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Miranda Reads" href="/user/show/71848701-miranda-reads">Miranda Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/71848701-miranda-reads?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/71848701-miranda-reads?shelf=ya-series">ya-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/71848701-miranda-reads?shelf=2018-finer-books-club-reading-chall">2018-finer-books-club-reading-chall</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2253667910" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14070135022794542450"><b> I desperately need a sequel to this prequel</b><br/><br/> Every one of them was just fabulous - seriously! <br/><br/>While there aren't any major spoilers, you won't appreciate these short stories without finishing the series. <b>Nearly every story is based on a key event</b> mentioned in one of our 8 main character's backgrounds.<br/><br/><b>The keeper</b> - This is the earliest prequel of the series - we follow Scarlet's Grandmother as she travels to Lunar as a young army piolet and meets a strange doctor. This doctor avoids using glamours</span>
  <span id="freeText14070135022794542450" style="display:none"><b> I desperately need a sequel to this prequel</b><br /><br /> Every one of them was just fabulous - seriously! <br /><br />While there aren't any major spoilers, you won't appreciate these short stories without finishing the series. <b>Nearly every story is based on a key event</b> mentioned in one of our 8 main character's backgrounds.<br /><br /><b>The keeper</b> - This is the earliest prequel of the series - we follow Scarlet's Grandmother as she travels to Lunar as a young army piolet and meets a strange doctor. This doctor avoids using glamours and quickly charms Scarlet's grandmother - nine months later, Scarlet's father was born. Years later, the same doctor comes to earth, carrying the broken body of toddler-Cinder - begging for her to hide the little girl. <br /><br /><b>Glitches</b> - Continuing from the last prequel, we get to see Cinder's story from the moment her hardware is installed to her adopted father contracts the plague. While I still think her stepmother and Pearl are ridiculously over-the-top with their cyborg hatred, I have a better understanding of where they're coming from. Plus, Iko makes an appearance - I adore her!<br /><br /><b>The Queen's Army</b> - We <b><i>finally</i> </b> get a story from Wolf's perspective! We learn about how he "joined" the army and a bit of the background of the mental manipulating and emotional struggles he went through. Until this story, I almost forgot Wolf even had a brother - though now I do understand why they had such animosity in the second novel.<br /><br /><b>Carswell's guide to being lucky</b> - A cute story about a devious and scheming Thorne. In the third book, Cress cites a myriad of reasons why she loves Thorne. One of her reasons was the basis of this story. I definitely prefer cool and suave adult-Thorne but it was certainly fun to see what his teenage years were like!<br /><br /><b>After sunshine passes by</b> - Here we get a bit of history about shell treatment and why Cress became so isolated. While I adore Cress, I much prefer her older persona when compared with her younger-self. <br /><br /><b>The princess and the guard</b> - A really sweet look into Winter and Jacin's shared childhood. We hear about why Winter never uses her Lunar gift but I never truly understood this until now. It's a wonder that not all of these Lunars are insane.<br /><br /><b>The little android</b> - This is a retelling of the Little Mermaid (and unsurprisingly, I was unhappy with the ending). Much like Iko, other androids sometimes experience personality 'glitches' that often mark them for disassembly. One little android escapes in time - and suddenly the whole world is open to her.<br /><br /><b>The mechanic</b> - The cute-meet from Prince Kai's perspective. Spoiler: it was a-freaking-dorable. Especially because we already know all the panic that was running through Cinder's mind. For once he seemed princely and not deer-in-the-headlights when people talk politics. <br /><br /><b>Something old, something new</b> - One lucky pair from the gang get marrrrried! It was sugary sweet and I delighted in it. I do wish there was more of a plot - but these characters have suffered enough and deserve one pleasant adventure.<br /><br /><b>Audiobook Comments</b><br />Well-read, though sometimes the audio would take on a different tone in the middle of the paragraph/sentence - almost like it was re-recorded and inserted at a later date. Anyone else notice this or was it just my digital copy?<br /><br /><i>The Finer Books Club - 2018 Reading Challenge: A prequel </i><br /><br /><a href="http://bit.ly/33ii2CT" rel="nofollow noopener">YouTube</a> | <a href="http://www.mirandareads.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/miranda.reads/?hl=en" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/Miranda_Reads" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | Snapchat @miranda.reads <br /><br />Happy Reading!</span>
  <a data-text-id="14070135022794542450" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1548715046" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1548715046" />
    <a title="Emily May" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may"><img alt="Emily May" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528390751p2/4622890.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1548715046?book_show_action=true">Feb 14, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emily May" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emily May" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may">Emily May</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=2016">2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=short-stories">short-stories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=fairy-tales">fairy-tales</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1548715046" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11708811797034838648">2 1/2 stars. I was disappointed with this collection. It works as a way of giving us fangirls and fanboys something to read while waiting for <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18584855.Heartless' title='Heartless by Marissa Meyer' rel='nofollow noopener'>Heartless</a>, but the stories don't really add anything.<br/><br/>Aside from one story - <i>The Little Android</i> - it's almost a stretch to call these "short stories". They are all little snippets, filling in the blanks behind the main story of The Lunar Chronicles and never really taking us to new places. Of course, this book is meant for the fans and it reunites us with o</span>
  <span id="freeText11708811797034838648" style="display:none">2 1/2 stars. I was disappointed with this collection. It works as a way of giving us fangirls and fanboys something to read while waiting for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18584855.Heartless" title="Heartless by Marissa Meyer" rel="nofollow noopener">Heartless</a>, but the stories don't really add anything.<br /><br />Aside from one story - <i>The Little Android</i> - it's almost a stretch to call these "short stories". They are all little snippets, filling in the blanks behind the main story of The Lunar Chronicles and never really taking us to new places. Of course, this book is meant for the fans and it reunites us with our favourite characters, but the stories aren't new or surprising. <br /><br /><i>The Keeper</i> tells the tale of Michelle Benoit and how she receives and looks after Cinder. It also shows Scarlet growing up with her grandmother. Do we learn anything new? Is there an interesting spin to this story (which we already know about anyway)? Do the characters change in our eyes? Nope. <br /><br /><i>Glitches</i> is Cinder's story as she arrives at her stepmother's house and tries to find her place. <i>The Queen’s Army</i> is about how Wolf becomes a soldier. <b>We know this already</b>. We don't learn anything new or gain new perspective. I never felt like I was discovering anything I hadn't already read about in the main series.<br /><br />Even the last story - <i>Something Old, Something New</i> - which tags an epilogue onto the main story arc of the series, really just tells the tale of what is implied by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13206900.Winter__The_Lunar_Chronicles___4_" title="Winter (The Lunar Chronicles, #4) by Marissa Meyer" rel="nofollow noopener">Winter</a>'s ending. A better title might have been <i>The Happy Ending, Pt 2</i>.<br /><br />It's good that I like these characters enough to care about their basic interactions and back stories, otherwise my rating would probably be lower. Also, <i>The Little Android</i> deserves some credit for being an imaginative retelling of <i>The Little Mermaid</i> and easily the most interesting story here.<br /><br /><a href="http://thebookgeek.org" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.facebook.com/thebookgeekreviews" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/thebookgeek01" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://instagram.com/emleemay" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/c/EmilyMayTheBookGeek" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a href="https://society6.com/bookgeek/" rel="nofollow noopener">Store</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="11708811797034838648" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText14351366682956822782" style="display:none"><b>Re-Read through audio! I have one more to go and I will have re-read - er, listened to the entire series and it's still one of my favorite series ever!</b><br><br>MY BLOG: <a href="http://melissa413readsalot.blogspot.com/2016/02/stars-above-by-marissa-meyer.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Melissa Martin's Reading List</a><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454506252ra/17972732.gif" alt=" " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>♥ OH STARS ABOVE! I LOVE YOU DEAR BOOK! ♥</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454506252ra/17972733.gif" alt=" " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book is soooooooo good! Some of the stories we have heard before, but they are still great.<b>I'm not going to go into each little tale, I do want to add things from a few of them.</b> All of the Lunar Chronicle fans should love this book. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454034089i/17907377._SX540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>THE KEEPER</u>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454534555ra/17978515.gif" alt=" " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In this story we find out when Cinder was brought to be watched over in her suspended animation tank and it also intertwined with Scarlet's story. <br><br>Scarlet is only seven-years-old when she comes to live with her grandmother Michelle. As these are short stories, it tells of her growing up at different ages. <br><br><b>---&gt;EXCERPT&lt;---</b><br><br><b>
  <i>Scarlet loved her grandmother for her quirks, but even she found it a little off-putting to receive a weapon-an actual, deadly weapon-for her eleventh birthday. Sure, she'd used the shotgun before to chase away wild wolves or shoot clay pigeons when she was bored. But a handgun? This wasn't for hunting. This was for...protection.</i>
</b><br><br>Like I said, I enjoyed them all but I'm just naming a few so don't look for these to be in any order. <br><br><b>
  <u>THE QUEEN'S ARMY</u>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454534555i/17978516._SX540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This one goes into detail about when Z (Ze've Kesley) was taken into the queen's army to become one of her wolf men. <br><br><b>---&gt;EXCERPT&lt;---</b><br><br><b>
  <i>They said the anesthesia would give him such a deep, empty sleep that there would be no dreams, but they were wrong. He dreamed of needles burrowing into this skin. He dreamed of pliers gripping his teeth. He dreamed of hot ashes and smoke in his eyes. He dreamed of a white tundra, a cold he had never known and a hunger barely satisfied by dripping meat in his jaws.</i>
</b><br><br><br><b>
  <u>AFTER SUNSHINE PASSES BY</u>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454534555i/17978517._SX540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This one tells about sweet little Cress. When she was little she so wanted to impress the queen and become recognized for more than a shell. But, we all know that didn't happen, this tells of her journey to her little station as a young girl. It's sad :-( <br><br><b>---&gt;EXCERPT&lt;---</b><br><br><b>
  <i>Her gaze reattached to Earth. It reminded her of a lullaby one of the older girls had taught her years ago, one that Cress still loved to sing to the children at lights-out.<br><br>Sweet Crescent Moon, up in the sky, <br>Won't you sing your song to Earth as she passes by?<br>Your sweetest silver melody, a rhythm and a rhyme, <br>A lullaby of pleasant dreams as you make your climb. <br>Send the forests off to bed, the mountains tuck in tight, <br>Rock the ocean gently, and the deserts kiss good night. <br>Sweet Crescent Moon, up in the sky, <br>You sing your song so sweetly after sunshine passes by.</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <u>THE PRINCESS AND THE GUARD</u>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454534555ra/17978518.gif" alt=" " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This story is about Winter and her sweet guard Jacin Clay. It's so sweet them playing as children. It also tells in great detail of how the evil queen Levana marred Winter's face. I hate her! and I hate her some more! <br><br><b>---&gt;EXCERPT&lt;---</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"Help me, Sir Clay! Save me!" Winter cowered behind the fort pillows. Though their fortress was strong, she knew it would not keep out the villains forever. <br>Luckily, at the most opportune of moments, Sir Jacin Clay leaped to her defense, brandishing the legendary Earthlight Saber-in reality, a wooden training sword he'd gotten from his father for his seventh birthday.</i>
</b><br><br>I loved all of the beautiful stories in the book. I devoured each little tidbit from this beautiful series I love so much. If you haven't read it yet... READ IT :-) <br><br>I look forward to Marissa Meyer's new book, Heartless!</span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1669484497" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1669484497" />
    <a title="Nat" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23381142-nat"><img alt="Nat" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1588309995p2/23381142.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1669484497?book_show_action=true">Jun 15, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nat" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nat" href="/user/show/23381142-nat">Nat</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23381142-nat?shelf=short-stories">short-stories</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1669484497" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9098211438716615782"><b>Update: I accidentally deleted my original review, so I had to upload it again.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1466013908ra/19428845.gif' width='340' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>This review contains <b>*spoilers*</b>.<br/><br/>I had to take a few hours off from my life after I finished this book so I could recover enough to review it.<br/>When I read <b> Winter </b>back in November I had prepared myself to say goodbye to the wonderful characters in this book. The closer I got to that dreadful last page the longer I tried to make it last- I realized that I was not ready to say goodbye and was immensely grateful when I fou</span>
  <span id="freeText9098211438716615782" style="display:none"><b>Update: I accidentally deleted my original review, so I had to upload it again.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1466013908ra/19428845.gif" width="340" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This review contains <b>*spoilers*</b>.<br><br>I had to take a few hours off from my life after I finished this book so I could recover enough to review it.<br>When I read <b> Winter </b>back in November I had prepared myself to say goodbye to the wonderful characters in this book. The closer I got to that dreadful last page the longer I tried to make it last- I realized that I was not ready to say goodbye and was immensely grateful when I found out that I wouldn't have to separate from my favorite series for another few months because <i>Stars Above</i> was coming out.<br>But now that it’s here, it’s even harder to say goodbye. The characters in this book all have a special place in my heart and I’m (still) so, so grateful that nobody died.<br><br>Ratings for each of the stories:<br><br><u>The Keeper</u>: <b>4.5/5 stars</b><br><i>“Cinders. Embers. Ashes. Michelle hoped that whatever strength had allowed this child to survive the fire all those years ago was a strength that still burned inside her. That it would go on burning, hotter and hotter, until she was as bright as the rising sun.”</i><br><br>Stars, I loved loved loved reading more about Michelle Benoit. When we first heard about her in The Lunar Chronicles I instantly wanted to know more (about her mission to Luna, her relationship with Logan, her relationship with Scarlet…).<br>And little baby Scarlet was adorable I kept imagining her with one of her front teeth missing and it’s just too cute. Scarlet is one of my favorite characters from this series. She is brave, sweet, strong and I will always want to know more about her.<br><br><i>“The train entered a new station and she squeezed her backpack against her side and tried to look grouchy as new passengers boarded. She exuded her best “leave me alone” vibes.”</i><br>Scarlet on that train ride was 100% me.<br><br><u>Glitches</u>: <b>4/5 stars</b><br><i>“I have a glitch, too. Sometimes I forget that I’m not human. I don’t think that happens to most androids.”</i><br><br>I read this short story right after I finished reading <b>Winter</b>, so this was a reread for me— and it’s still as good as I remembered it to be.<br><i>Glitches</i> explains how Cinder came to live with Adri and the girls and how she didn't remember anything of her previous life. It was heartbreaking, and it definitely worked to increase my love of Peony, Iko, and Cinder. I missed these characters so much.<br><br><i>"Who’s Prince Kai?”<br>Peony spun toward her so fast, she tripped on the skirts of Adri’s kimono and fell, screaming, onto her bed. “Who’s Prince Kai?” she yelled, struggling to sit back up. “Only my future husband! Honestly, don’t girls in Europe know about him?”</i><br><br><u>The Queen's Army</u>: <b>4/5 stars</b><br><i>"He would be brave—so his brother would not see his fear. He would be strong for him."</i><br><br>This story was also a reread for me and I forgot just how much I loved Wolf.<br>It was interesting having a little bit of background on him because I always want to know more about my favorite characters. <i>The Queen’s Army</i> was definitely on the darker side- the whole concept of Levana’s army is so terrifying. And watching the army take Wolf from his family made me tear up.<br><br><u>Carswell’s Guide to Being Lucky</u>: <b>4/5 stars</b><br>Oh, Captain Thorne, how I missed you.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1466014307ra/19428885.gif" width="460" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is a super fun and quick read that I giggled at in a few places (only Carswell can make me giggle).<br>This story was actually mentioned in <b> Cress</b>— when Captain Thorne and Cress talk about how young Carswell defended a girl and then got suspended for it.<br>It was really interesting seeing the actions of a younger Thorne, and it honestly made my heart grow even fonder of him.<br><br><u>After Sunshine Passes By</u>: <b>4/5 stars</b><br><i>“Sweet Crescent Moon, up in the sky,<br>You sing your song so sweetly after sunshine passes by.”</i><br><br>This is the story of how Sybil placed Crescent Moon in that horrible satellite. Cress is such a sweet character and I had tears in my eyes when she thought that Sybil was going to take her somewhere nice to reward her for all of her hard work.<br><br><i>“She’d been so focused on going to Earth. So excited about trees and oceans and cities …<br>And now she didn’t have any of that. She didn’t even have the dormitory or the other shells anymore.”</i><br><br><u>The Princess and the Guard</u>: <b>4.5/5 stars</b><br>I’m in love with Jacin’s love for Winter.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422154220ra/13463875.gif" width="450" height="225" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>"There was no safe place. Not in Artemisia. Not on all of Luna.<br>Except—Jacin.<br>When her screams succumbed to hysterical sobbing, Jacin finally allowed his hold to turn from the grip of a jailer to the embrace of her best friend.<br>“This is why,” he whispered, and it occurred to Winter that, at some point, he’d started crying too. “This is why I can’t leave you, Winter. This is why I’ll never leave.”</i><br><br>In this story we discover in depth why Winter decided to not use her Lunar gift.<br>A part of this was mentioned in the book <b>Winter</b>, when the servant tried to kill herself and Winter "saved" her by using her Lunar gift. But then the princess finds out why the servant had wanted to jump of the edge- and she vows to never use her gift again.<br>This is where I got really emotional.<br><br><i>“Winter’s entire world was spinning and it occurred to her with sudden clarity that this was wrong. Her training sessions. The thaumaturges. The entire Lunar gift. The power that the strong, like she and the queen and Aimery, held over the weak. Like this servant girl. Like Jacin.<br>Like Winter’s father.”</i><br><br><u>The Mechanic</u>: <b>4/5 stars</b><br><i>“The mechanic?”<br>The girl—Cinder—nodded. “How can I help you?”<br>Kai stared at the top of her head.<br>Linh Cinder.<br>The renown. The reputation. The approval rating.<br>New Beijing’s best mechanic was … a teenager?”</i><br><br>It’s been almost a year since I first read <b>Cinder</b>, so I’d forgotten how cute Kai and Cinder were when they first met.<br>And Iko had me laughing so hard I had tears in my eyes, I love her!<br><br><i>“Iko, please pay your respects to our customer … His Imperial Highness.<br>The android’s sensor flashed as she scanned Kai’s face. “Prince Kai,” she said, her voice taking on the unexpected tinge of a sigh. “You are even more handsome in person.”<br>Kai laughed—a sudden, uncontrollable laugh that burst out of him before he could reel it back.”</i><br><br><u>Something Old, Something New</u>: <b>5/5 stars</b><br><i>“I wanted a quiet, intimate wedding, not a circus.”<br>Thorne leaned against the staircase rail. “It’s the first known Lunar-Earthen wedding in generations, the groom is a bioengineered wolf-human hybrid, and you invited the emperor of the Eastern Commonwealth and an ex–Lunar Queen. What did you expect?”<br>Scarlet glared at him. “I am marrying the man that I love, and I invited my friends to celebrate with us. I expected a little bit of privacy.”</i><br><br>Wolf and Scarlet are getting MARRIED. I had no idea that they were getting married. THANK YOU Marissa Meyer for that pleasant surprise. Scarlet and Wolf are one of my favorite couples from this series and they are getting married. I’m still freaking out.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427890375ra/14330928.gif" width="290" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>“Oh, Scarlet,” Cress sighed. “You’re getting married. It’s all like a dream.”<br>“I guess it sort of is,” Scarlet agreed, her cheeks flushing pink around her freckles.”</i><br><br>I missed them all so much. I love Thorne and Cress and Scarlet and Wolf and Cinder and Iko and Kai and Winter and Jacin. I’m in love with all of them.<br><br><i>“Hey, Cinder,” Thorne said, pacing to the opening that separated the entryway from a humble sitting room. “Remember when we were here before? When we were just two crazy fugitives, on the run from the law?”</i><br><br>Yes Thorne, I do remember- don’t make me cry harder.<br><br>And the reunion between them all- ahhh I couldn’t handle it. I love Marissa Meyer for writing it so beautifully.<br><br><i>“I told them that was the dulcet roar of a Rampion’s engines,” said Kai, “but they all insisted it was just another media hover flying over.”<br>Cinder crossed her arms over her chest. “You’re an expert on the sound levels of spaceships now, are you?”<br>“Nah,” said Kai. “I’ve just been waiting to hear that sound all day.”<br>She smiled at him, feeling the hummingbird flutter of her own pulse. He smiled back.<br>“Aces,” said Thorne with a low groan. “They haven’t even kissed yet and they’re already making me nauseous.”</i><br><br>Oh, how I missed Thorne’s snarky remarks.<br>I can’t even begin to explain how happy <b>Something Old, Something New</b> made me, it was the most beautiful impromptu wedding ever created.<br><br><i>“Wolf took a step closer so that he towered over Scarlet, creating what could have been a moment of intimacy if the room hadn’t been so crowded. “So? Will you marry me?”<br>Scarlet started to smile.<br>“Wait. Before you answer that,” said Thorne, gesturing around the room, “you should know that the store where we got all this stuff doesn’t take returns.”<br>Casting her gaze skyward, Scarlet said, “Well, in that case. Yes. Yes, of course I will.”</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1399901324ra/9607775.gif" width="500" height="270" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Also, I finally found out the answer to my most pressing question in an interview <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/childrens-books-site/2016/feb/02/marissa-meyer-lunar-chronicles-interview" rel="nofollow noopener">The Guardian</a> did with Marissa Meyer:<br><b>Are the characters of Thorne and Cress in any way inspired by Flynn and Rapunzel from the Disney movie Tangled?</b><br><br><i>Surprisingly, no! I had actually completed the first draft of <b>Cress</b> before Tangled came out, and I remember going to see the movie in theaters and having a jaw-dropping moment and thinking: Hey, that’s my cocky bandit thief! There are so many examples of similar things cropping up in the same time in our culture or media, and this was definitely one of them. It’s so weird how that happens!</i><br><br><i>*Note: I'm an Amazon Affiliate. If you're interested in buying</i> <b>Stars Above</b>, <i>just click on the image below to go through my link. I'll make a small commission!*</i><br><a target="_blank" href="https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1250091845/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=9325&amp;creativeASIN=1250091845&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;tag=natalie013-20&amp;linkId=b2aa4e0f9c312b8cd192cb8b635c4192" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1482936381i/21563663.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1482936381i/21563664.gif" width="1" height="1" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="https://bookspoils.wordpress.com" rel="nofollow noopener">This review and more can be found on my blog.</a></span>

  <span id="freeText10502050361106562994" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>"The room was full of white crepe paper and tulle, unburned candles and glass lanterns, streamers and small silk bags overflowing with sugared almonds.<br><br>Iko gasped and trailed a finger over an enormous tulle bow. "Is this all for the wedding?"</i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1459072177ra/18565697.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ah, the wedding. Admit it, nine and three quarters of you bought Stars Above just to see who's getting hitched. <br><br>I enjoyed it less than I thought it would, but it has nothing to do with the characters chosen. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Kudos to Meyer for not picking Kai and Cinder. Cress and Thorne are my favorite couple and I wish it'd been them, but Scarlet/Wolf come a close second in my heart. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> It has a distinct drabble feel with too little substance. <br><br>My favorite story by far is The Princess and the Guard, Winter and Jacin's story. She enters late in the series, so we never find out as much about her as the rest of the gang. In it, we see Winter before she goes mad and the exact scene Levana forces her to mutilate herself. The reason she does it is different than the original books led me to believe and I'm glad Meyer let us see a little deeper into Levana and Winter's relationship.<br><br>The rest aren't as good, I'm afraid. Three (Glitches, The Queen's Army, and The Little Android) have already been published a long time ago on Meyer's <a href="https://www.wattpad.com/user/marissameyer22" rel="nofollow noopener">Wattpad</a> and Carswell's Guide to Getting Lucky is provided when you sign up for her newsletter. They're free and don't provide much extra information, but I did mention they're free, right, so who cares? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1459072177ra/18565698.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The Keeper (Scarlet's grandmother's story) and After Sunshine Passes By (Cress's story) don't tell us anything we don't already get from the main series. The Mechanic is basically a short rewrite of Cinder from Kai's POV. I've never shipped them anyway and it leans towards fanservice.<br><br>The Little Android, even though I'd read it before, affected me just as much as last time. It's a retelling of The Little Android and absolutely beautiful and heartbreaking. I reviewed it <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/900361984" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a> and I strongly urge you to read it on Wattpad if you're a little strapped for cash. It's free. I just want to emphasize that. <i>Freeeeee</i>. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1459072316ra/18565741.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Do I recommend Stars Above? Eh. If you're a super, super fan and want the set. Other than that, it's pretty much a gorgeous cover holding lots of cream and too little cake.<br><br><br><br><b>Pre-review:</b> Does the tiara come with the book? ;)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448954581ra/17213253.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="10502050361106562994" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47627265-kaylin-the-re-read-queen?shelf=short-stories">short-stories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47627265-kaylin-the-re-read-queen?shelf=memorable-male-characters">memorable-male-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47627265-kaylin-the-re-read-queen?shelf=recommended-to-me">recommended-to-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47627265-kaylin-the-re-read-queen?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47627265-kaylin-the-re-read-queen?shelf=favorite-female-characters">favorite-female-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47627265-kaylin-the-re-read-queen?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1992044144" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14926925238911960025"><b> 4 Stars </b><br/><br/>(It actually averaged out to like 3.2 but I loved some of these so much I’m rounding up)<br/><br/><b>The Keeper</b><br/><br/>4/5 <br/><br/>This story focuses on Michelle Benoit and her role in saving Princess Selene; all things referenced in the original series. However, I really enjoyed seeing how it all played out, and young Scarlet was a delight. <br/><br/><b>Glitches</b><br/><br/>2/5<br/><br/>Young Cinder meeting her new family (and of course, wicked stepmother) was actually really boring. We’re already aware of how awful Ardi is. We’re aware of Cinder an</span>
  <span id="freeText14926925238911960025" style="display:none"><b> 4 Stars </b><br><br>(It actually averaged out to like 3.2 but I loved some of these so much I’m rounding up)<br><br><b>The Keeper</b><br><br>4/5 <br><br>This story focuses on Michelle Benoit and her role in saving Princess Selene; all things referenced in the original series. However, I really enjoyed seeing how it all played out, and young Scarlet was a delight. <br><br><b>Glitches</b><br><br>2/5<br><br>Young Cinder meeting her new family (and of course, wicked stepmother) was actually really boring. We’re already aware of how awful Ardi is. We’re aware of Cinder and Peony’s friendship. This was all stuff we’d seen before. Some of the backstory and explanations for Cinder’s cyborg pieces were interesting, though. <br><br><b>Queen’s Army</b><br><br>5/5<br><br>Baby <s>Wolf</s> Ze’ev is precious. This was a really interesting character study I wish had been explored more in the initial series. I liked seeing the pack dynamics, and I still think it’s weird Ze’ev’s brother isn’t even mentioned outside of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13206760.Scarlet__The_Lunar_Chronicles___2_" title="Scarlet (The Lunar Chronicles, #2) by Marissa Meyer" rel="nofollow noopener">Scarlet</a>. This expanded upon their relationship and I found it really interesting. <br><br><b>Carswell’s Guide to Being Lucky</b><br><br>5/5<br><br>I’m Thorne trash #1, so did you really expect anything different? He’s such a fun character, even when scaled back to an obnoxious 13-year-old. I enjoyed seeing the Kate incident as it actually was, instead of both the versions Thorne and Cress painted in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13206828.Cress__The_Lunar_Chronicles___3_" title="Cress (The Lunar Chronicles, #3) by Marissa Meyer" rel="nofollow noopener">Cress</a>.<br><br><b>After Sunshine Passes BY</b><br><br>2/5<br><br>I was really, really, really bored. I like Cress’ character—I really do! I think she’s crazy smart and funny, and I enjoy seeing what she brings to the table. But baby-Cress’ childhood was lonely and boring. I knew this already, I didn’t need to <i>see</i> just how boring and lonely it was. <br><br><b>The Princess and the Guard</b><br><br>3.5/5<br><br>Winter and Jacin are just great. I love their dynamic together and seeing how it evolved from childhood. Winter especially is a really fascinating character to me, and seeing how she became the crazy mess we met in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13206900.Winter__The_Lunar_Chronicles___4_" title="Winter (The Lunar Chronicles, #4) by Marissa Meyer" rel="nofollow noopener">Winter</a> was great. My main problem is it implies Jacin gave up on his dreams for Winter—when that’s not how it’s painted in the original story? Wasn’t Jacin supposed to start an internship, and Levanna forced him into being a guard? <br><s>Did I completely misunderstand that?</s><br><br><b>The Little Android</b><br><br>1/5<br><br>This was soooo long. And sooo boring. It tried to create a whole new world and cast of characters in order to incorporate The Little Mermaid into this universe. But it needed to be it’s own story so it had time to develop, instead this felt really overstuffed and I didn’t care about anyone. Plus, this whole book is supposed to be filled with extra’s from TLC… and this featured none of the characters or anything about it?<br><br><b>The Mechanic</b><br><br>2/5<br><br>Two stars for Kai because he is precious. No stars for seeing the exact same scene I’ve already seen before. I didn’t think this scene was particularly interesting the first time around. They way Kai and Cinder’s relationship develops is great, but the beginning is so cliché-Cinderella… I just don’t care for it. <br><br><b>Something Old, Something New</b><br><br>5+/5<br><br>*screaming*<br><br>I NEED LIKE SIX SEQUELS TO THIS PLEASE. <br><br>IT’S SO CUTE AND EVERYONE'S DEVELOPMENT AND RELATIONSHIPS ARE GREAT. IT’S SO MUCH FUN AND EVERYONE IS SO STRONG AND HAPPY AND I’M STILL HAVING A LOT OF EMOTIONS.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1481733578ra/21450104.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="14926925238911960025" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

But I still can't keep myself from hoping for more.   <span id="freeText16004107104915241666" style="display:none"><i>“I will accept any amount of monsters my mind wants to give me, but I will not become a monster myself.”</i><br /><br />I guess and I dread that this is the last we will hear from the Lunar Chronicles. But I still can't keep myself from hoping for more. Apparantly there's going to be a series of graphic novels, though, featuring Iko as the main character.<br /><br />It was so amazing returning to this science fiction/fantasy universe, to all my beloved characters, to their bantering and giggling and being actual cinnamon rolls.<br />While some shorts didn't amaze or surprise me much, I could still enjoy them a lot. But what did it for me were the heartbreaking story of <i>The little Android</i>,Carswell's Chapter and the final happily ever after. The three shorts were new and surprising, funny and witty, smart and overall just exactly what I wished for.<br /><br /><a href="https://www.instagram.com/fantasticbooksandwheretofindem/" rel="nofollow noopener">Find more of my books on Instagram</a></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1398504136?book_show_action=true">Sep 22, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kainat 《HUFFLEPUFF &amp; PROUD》" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kainat 《HUFFLEPUFF &amp; PROUD》" href="/user/show/14717996-kainat-hufflepuff-proud">Kainat 《HUFFLEPUFF &amp; PROUD》</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1398504136" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14027116492460508243">Rereading because a certain someone is making me feel all the feels! <br/><br/><b>6 Stars!! ★ ★ ★ ★ ★ ★<br/></b><p>
  <i>《《"And they all lived happily ever after"》》</i>
</p> <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462677762i/19029258._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> The Epilogue.★ ★ ★ ★ ★ </b><br/><i>
  <b>"... I think she was a little concerned that i never made very many friends. And now look. I have so many friends, i need a cargo ship to keep you all in." </b>
</i> <-- AWWW!<br/><br/>It was everything and more!! It was the closure i didn't know i needed! I still find myself randomly hugging this book, or just reading the bits of it when I'm bored. I</span>
  <span id="freeText14027116492460508243" style="display:none">Rereading because a certain someone is making me feel all the feels! <br><br><b>6 Stars!! ★ ★ ★ ★ ★ ★<br></b><p>
  <i>《《"And they all lived happily ever after"》》</i>
</p> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462677762i/19029258._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> The Epilogue.★ ★ ★ ★ ★ </b><br><i>
  <b>"... I think she was a little concerned that i never made very many friends. And now look. I have so many friends, i need a cargo ship to keep you all in." </b>
</i> &lt;-- AWWW!<br><br>It was everything and more!! It was the closure i didn't know i needed! I still find myself randomly hugging this book, or just reading the bits of it when I'm bored. I'm so glad we got this epilogue, i broke into tears many times, not the sad tears, not the angry tears, but happy tears! I didn't even know there was a such a thing. This series will always have a special place in my heart. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436131602ra/15422438.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>The Keeper. ★ ★ ★ </b><br>I love little Scarlet, she is so brave! No wonder she despised her father in the 2nd book. There was this part when Scarlet mentioned having a crush on some guy in her class, i was like..<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454893798ra/18026898.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Glitches.</b> (Get it?) <b>★ ★ ★</b><br><i>"She raised her finger to the corner of her right eye, <br>searching for wetness that wasn't there.<br>'Right. A glitch. Maybe that's all it is.'"</i> <br><br>I love this title. This one gave me the feels! I never really cared about Cinder as much as others but this made me want to go back and reread the first book with a new respect for her. <br><br><b>The Queen's Army. ★ ★ ★</b><br><i>“'Please,' he said, wrapping his arms around his mother's waist. If he held on tight on enough, they could never force him to let go. <b>He clamped his eyes shut as the first hot tears slipped out</b>. 'Please don't let them__'”</i><br><br>Wolf, Wolf, my baby Wolf! This one was the hardest to read for me. I hate Levana is all i have to say! <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454894654ra/18026995.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Carswell's Guide to being Lucky. ★ ★ ★ ★ ★</b><br><i>"Carswell stifled a sigh. Maybe he could start an after-school Flirting 101 class. There were a lot of people in this school who could really use the help."</i><br> <br>Carswell Thorne, at the age of 12, is a flirt and a con artist. He uses his charms to steal smarter kids' math homework. I can't with him, where i was devastated for other kids, he made me laugh! Please don't hate me, but i ship him with Kate so hard! In my head she is still Cress, just with brown eyes. <br><br><b>After Sunshine Passes By. ★ ★ ★ ★ </b><br><i>"She would sing for a while before she began her work. Singing always made her feel better. <br><b> Sweet Crescent moon, up i the sky...,</b><br>That was all she could get through before the tears came in earnest, drowning out everything else."</i><br><br>Ohh little Cress! This was heartbreaking! Especially reading this right after Thorne's. Little Cress wants Syblil to be proud of her and she would do anything to make her happy. This is just too much.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1421108215ra/13323534.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>The princess and the Guard. ★ ★ ★ ★</b><br><i>"She didn't even consider using her glamour to hide the three gashes and the blood that dripped down her neck, staining her dress. She was proud. Her wound was proof that she had been to battle and survived."</i><br><br>This one is a must read! Back when Jain wasn't so cold, and Winter wasn't crazy, they were just two kids, and they were fucking adorable! I teared up multiple times while reading this. This explains so much, how she went crazy, why she decided not to use her gift, how she got her scars, and her hallucinations. Their friendship/love is legendary! I love them so freaking much. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395339549ra/8982005.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>The Little Android. ★ ★ ★</b><br>Okay, WHAT. THE. FUCK. DID. I. JUST. READ? How the hell these robots are developing human emotions? It's creepy as hell. This was so sad... i cried her her? It? What was that? I do not know but what i do know is, it was B E A U T I F U L. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454920286ra/18028472.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>The Mechanic. ★ ★ ★ ★ ★</b><br><i>"If i'm not back in an hour, then i've probably been cornered by paparazzi and screaming girs and you should send the royal security squad after me."</i><br><br>This was the one i wanted to read the most, and it did not disappoint me! If anything it was too short. I could read the whole book from Kai's POV. You know how Jain and Wolf are super intense, and Thorne is a player.. Kai is just so nice without being boring, it's just so rare. I love him! I want more. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454923389ra/18028899.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>02-05-2016</b><br><b>Where the fuck is my copy, Amazon? It was supposed to arrive on the 2nd! Never trusting you again, EVER!</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403247772ra/10064494.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>To all my Lunar babies...</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451783786ra/17604610.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1304013927" />
    <a title="Mara" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10194700-mara"><img alt="Mara" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1599132109p2/10194700.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1304013927?book_show_action=true">Jun 10, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mara" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mara" href="/user/show/10194700-mara">Mara</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1304013927" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12405745366358169833">Perfectly selected and strung together short story collection that will have any Lunar Chronicles fan emotionally drained upon finishing. Beautifully written, every single story had me euphoric from happiness and sense of adventure and wonder. Stars above, this was epic. (For people starting the series, I highly recommend reading this collection after finishing Winter.)</span>

          </span>
        </div>

So don't be surprised if my favourite stories list features practically all the stories but three or four.<br/><br/>So, <b>favourite stories</b>:<br/>•<b>

  </i>
</b> because THORNE.<br/>•<b>
  <i>After Sunshine Passes By </i>
</b>because LITTLE CRESS. I've alw</span>
  <span id="freeText12691563023151653933" style="display:none"><b>"But she was already vast and bright and endless."</b><br><br>It would be more logical to list the ones which are <i>not </i> my favourites, but, however cynical and pragmatic I may be, I always like to see the glass half-full. So don't be surprised if my favourite stories list features practically all the stories but three or four.<br><br>So, <b>favourite stories</b>:<br>•<b>
  <i>
    <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1413560120" rel="nofollow noopener">The Queen's Army</a>
  </i>
</b> because WOLF.<br>•<b>
  <i>
    <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1451866265" rel="nofollow noopener">Carswell's Guide to Being Lucky</a>
  </i>
</b> because THORNE.<br>•<b>
  <i>After Sunshine Passes By </i>
</b>because LITTLE CRESS. I've alway found so much of myself in her character that I can never help sympathizing with her, so much that this story almost brought me to the edge of tears.<br>•<b>
  <i>The Princess and the Guard</i>
</b> because Winter and Jacin's friendship is marvellous, and I loved how the author represented it through the metaphor of the games they used to play as children.<br>•<b>
  <i>The Little Android</i>
</b> because- wait, are those tears? Seriously, girl. Behave yourself.<br>•<b>
  <i>Something Old, Something New</i>
</b> because THE WEDDING. And you know what? It was exactly whose I hoped it would be! Me madly happy.<br><br>But I am one for equality, so a word or two also for the other novellas.<br>•<b>
  <i>The Keeper</i>
</b> is a really useful and interesting story about how Michelle's path crossed that of princess Selene and about Scarlet's childhood as well.<br>•<b>
  <i>
    <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1410222107" rel="nofollow noopener">Glitches</a>
  </i>
</b> tells about Cinder's early days in Linh's house, and you'd probably want to read it to see the birth of her friendhsip with Iko. Extremely cute.<br>•<b>
  <i>The Mechanic</i>
</b> is the first meeting between Cinder and Kai seen through his eyes. I thought I hated this kind of novellas written simply by someone else's point of view, but I actually enjoyed it a lot. It's called Meyer's effect.<br><br>If you're a fan of <i>The Lunar Chronicles</i> series, I honestly don't know what you're waiting for. Go read these novellas. I enjoyed them all, from the first to the last one, and even loved some. Higly recommended.<br><br><b>PRE-REVIEW</b><br>Uuuh, there'll be five inedited stories in this little jewel! <br>Well, let's see what we have: little Scarlet, little Cress, Winter and Jacin, Kai's pov of his first meeting with Cinder, the wedding of th-<br><br>Oh god. <br><br>Did I just read...? <br><br>"...<b>epilogue</b> to Winter, friends gather for the <b>wedding of the century</b>"<br><br>The wedding. of. the century. <br><br>The wedding of the century!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448973754ra/17216147.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="jesse&amp;#x1f4da;" class="user" itemprop="url" name="jesse&amp;#x1f4da;" href="/user/show/41640132-jesse-x1f4da">jesse&amp;#x1f4da;</a>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41640132-jesse-x1f4da?shelf=every-tear-is-a-waterfall">every-tear-is-a-waterfall</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1456928759" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5506142431852076198">CARSWELL FRICKEN THORNE AKA MY SWEET LITTLE CHILD I WANT TO CRADLE THIS BUNDLE OF HAPPINESS AND LULL HIM TO SLEEP BC HE’S LOVE<br/><br/><br/>Jesus Christ.<br/><br/>This is exactly what I needed.<br/><br/>FINALLY. A PROPER EPILOGUE TO <i>WINTER</i>.<br/><br/>I might have said this numerous times already but <i>Lunar Chronicles</i> is one of the very few series that’s so close to my heart. I didn’t exactly cry after <i>Winter</i> but I remember having such a heavy hangover because it has all <i>come to an end.</i><br/><br/>Oh my God I’m emotionally unstable.<br/><br/>The reason why I have</span>
  <span id="freeText5506142431852076198" style="display:none">CARSWELL FRICKEN THORNE AKA MY SWEET LITTLE CHILD I WANT TO CRADLE THIS BUNDLE OF HAPPINESS AND LULL HIM TO SLEEP BC HE’S LOVE<br /><br /><br />Jesus Christ.<br /><br />This is exactly what I needed.<br /><br />FINALLY. A PROPER EPILOGUE TO <i>WINTER</i>.<br /><br />I might have said this numerous times already but <i>Lunar Chronicles</i> is one of the very few series that’s so close to my heart. I didn’t exactly cry after <i>Winter</i> but I remember having such a heavy hangover because it has all <i>come to an end.</i><br /><br />Oh my God I’m emotionally unstable.<br /><br />The reason why I haven’t read this sooner, I think might have something to do with me so not wanting the series to end. Its just that I can convince myself that <i>”yeah? We still got <b>Stars Above</b>”</i>. And after reading so many books, I think its kind of proper to return to this world again for once and give one of my favorite series the love it deserves.<br /><br />Some stories didn’t quite feel good as the others but no matter how much I think the story would be bad (IF it’s not a Lunar Chronicles collection), I still enjoy <b>every single thing</b> because that’s just how I love everyone in this series. But DO NOT WORRY everything is strangely goooood.<br /><br />These break-downs are written sometime after I’m stable enough to write anything at all because I kind of had to look for each stories’ qualities and not being biased because this is one of my favorite series of all time.<br /><br />So below, you’ll find <i>quite</i> a sane review because I tried to be (with the exceptions for <i>Something Old, Something New</i> which review is not exactly a review because its basically paragraphs of me trying to put my shit together because at that moment my hand was shaking and I WAS SUCH AN EMOTIONAL WRECK I NEED MORE I’M SO SAD I DON’T WANT THE SERIES TO END and I literally wrote it with tears streaming down my face, <b>I’m serious</b>)<br /><br /><br /><br /><b>
  <u>The Keeper</u>
</b><br />This is a story about Michelle Benoit who juggles up between keeping the secret identity of Cinder (who’s apparently hidden in a bomb shelter) and the responsibility of caring for Scarlet. It gives me an insight of Scarlet’s life and how her father is horrible. Nothing really happened, but as a dedicated fan of TLC, I love to read about Scarlet’s backstory, how we explore her relationship with her grandmother and I could think of nothing more aside from the words <i>Well, its good to be back in this world</i>.<br /><br /><b>
  <u>Glitches</u>
</b><br /><i>Glitches</i> fascinates me. I love love Cinder and nothing excites me more than getting an insight on Cinder’s life before she was a mechanic, and the part where Garan caught the letumosis is quite emotional. Though I despise Adri and Pearl even more now, I <i>think</i> I could understand her for a little bit, though I still don’t get her hatred for cyborgs. Also this is one of the original short stories! I feel so left out that I haven’t read it before this :/<br /><br /><b>
  <u>The Queen’s Army</u>
</b><br />Now now there. Wolf is like one of my favorite characters in the entire series (though that might seem a little biased because I love almost all the main characters, but really, I love Wolf). I totally get it why some people won’t find this near appealing but this story gives me an insight about Wolf, what he’s going through, what he needed to do to actually earn his place. Though its of course, not in anywhere near perfect but it makes me actually <i>feel something</i> and I love it. Something is... intriguing about Wolf that captivated me from the first time I read about him. And we finally get to see a glimpse about his life before.<br /><br /><b>
  <u>Carswell’s Guide to Being Lucky</u>
</b><br />I love Thorne. Its all I could ever say. He was a narcissistic ass so full of himself in <i>Scarlet</i> but <i>Cress</i> gave everything I need to redeem his character for me and I ended up being a Carswell Thorne huge fan (especially after <i>Winter</i>). And because of that, I’m feeling nostalgic as hell and I didn’t even realize how much I miss reading about him until now. The story feels like a little snippet about his life and I totally get it if somesone said this one didn’t do much especially for someone who despises Thorne (believe me I know some people who do). It was a long time ago since I read TLC so I can’t remember anything about a Kate Fallow though her name rings a bell somewhere. But I personally think this is a fun read.<br /><br /><b>
  <u>After Sunshine Passes by</u>
</b><br />Well? That comes as a surprise, even for me. Before I read this, I’m pretty sure I would give all the stories a good rating because I just love the series so much (didn’t I say its my one of my favorite series of all time?). But this one felt too short and unpolished. The story starts too abruptly and ends too abruptly and the fact that this story actually consists of only 2 scenes altogether and would probably count for only a 10 minute clip is just <i>ugh</i>. Its a very very short read, even for a short story but it could easily be one chapter in an actual book. I could literally summarize everything in a sentence. I hate naive characters but after reading <i>Cress</i> somehow she’s the first naive character that I love and ended up not getting on my nerves. I mean I <i>love</i> Cress but she comes up as irritating for such a <i>short</i> short story for me.<br /><br /><b>
  <u>The Princess and the Guard</u>
</b><br />When I read <i>Winter</i> I wasn’t too emotionally attached to both Winter and Jacin, personally because I think I have been with Cinder and the rest of the gang for too long that I’m more attached to them so there are pretty much a small room for Winter and Jacin because we only read and know about them in the final book. I love Winter, I like Jacin but not so much, but my love for the other characters just surpasses that of both of them. But after reading this one, I can’t deny it. Winter and Jacin are <i>soooo cute</i>. I totally get it now the reason why Winter doesn’t want to use her glamours and seeing her and Jacin as kids... <i>Oh my God</i>. They’re so cute I want to keep them away from the world. <br /><br /><b>
  <u>The Little Android</u>
</b><br /><i>did I just <b>cry</b> on a story about a fucking Android?</i> YES THAT HAPPENED.<br />I totes have no idea whether it was just me being emotional or that the story is <i>that</i> sad but Marissa Meyer managed to make me CRY in a novella that’s an achievement she should be proud of.<br />I like the Disney version of <i>The Little Mermaid</i>, but I won’t count it as my favorite Disney classic. The original story is quite intriguing for me but the ending feels too forced (the thing about her going to the heavens? Nonsense.)<br />This novella has <i>tons</i> of similarities to the original <i>The Little Mermaid</i> you can actually <i>feel</i> the atmosphere of the retelling. I know the story is sad but something about it is just <i>too emotional</i>. I was just reading it til’ the end and I quite didn’t get the ending at first, but then I read it again. Long story short, I finally got the ending and I ended up crying and so sad. Some Marissa Meyer magic there. Its hard for me to feel attached to a novella. But this one didn’t just make me <i>feel</i> but it made me <i>shed a tear</i>.<br />I know that the rating of this specific novella is slightly lower than that of the other novellas but I feel like this one is quite strong even though its not directly tied to the original series. And I love it <i>so much</i> its easily one of my favorite novella retellings.<br /><br /><b>
  <u>The Mechanic</u>
</b><br />I can’t believe I totally forgot how funny this entire series is. Its not those contemporary books that make you out loud laughing. But it has been a long time ago since I read <i>Cinder</i> and I had totally forgotten how exactly awkward is Cinder and Kai’s first meeting. I was giggling throughout this entire novella but its just that I miss these characters so much.<br /><br /><b>
  <u>Something Old, Something New</u>
</b><br />AND A PROPER FINALE TO <i>WINTER</i>.<br /><br /><b>DID I CRY?<br />I SPENT HALF AN HOUR CONTEMPLATING EVERY SINGLE THING</b><br /><br />This. Is. The. Ending. We. All. Deserve.<br /><br />Oh my I’m so emotional.<br /><br />THAT’S IT. ALL IS DONE. EVERYONE IS HAPPY.<br /><br />I don’t want this series to end but they’re all so happy and I’m emotional I choked on my own tears because I laugh and I cry and I stress because this is BEAUTIFUL.<br /><br />I love everyone.<br /><br />And I’m sorry I can’t provide a sane review because whenever I think of this I feel insane.<br /><br />I don’t just love these characters so much I LIVE for them.<br /><br />And I’m babbling now. Maybe I should stop.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5506142431852076198" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
